I drove past Orange Theory Fitness about a thousand times before deciding to check it out. My mother was already a member and so I signed up for my first free class. From that class, I became instantly hooked! It has revolutionized my life in every aspect.

I am a law school student and finding time to workout, for me, was a challenge. OTF is a 1 hour, high intensity workout that produces results. I was looking for a workout that would get me cut and OTF has 100% delivered. Each workout is something new and wearing a heart rate monitor allows you to see your progress, on the screens, during your workout! Working out at OTF has changed my life in so many aspects. From the way I eat, the way I exercise, and the way I perform in the classroom/ court room!

The trainers are extremely motivating and personable. They really want to see you succeed and push you to your limit! The OTF Carmel Valley  staff has become like family! They are so friendly even at 5am!

If you are looking to challenge yourself and see fast results, OTF is your answer!<//review>

On December 7th at 10:30 at night I lost my precious 13 year old dog, a Chihuahua mix, Mona, who is blind, while walking my dogs in the desert in Cathedral City. I searched for over 14 hours.  It was the coldest night of the year.  There were fresh coyote tracks all over the desert.  My other dogs and I searched the whole desert and the the surrounding streets to no avail.

I was beside myself.  I love Mona so much.  After 14 hours I was devastated.  Mona can't even run.

Then, my prayers were answered.  Mona showed up on Petland's website after it was open only a few hours.

My deepest gratitude to the Animal Control Officer who found her!  Thank you!!!  She  had made it to the street.  It was a miracle the Animal Control Officer found her before she got hit.  She is blind.

I commend you for a job extremely well done!  You saved Mona's life, and for that I am eternally grateful!

The front desk lady and the gentleman who handled Mona while I was there were all very professional, yet compassionate.  I can't thank you all enough!<//text>

I've been to the shelter a number of times to look for just the right pup to adopt.  Every time I visited I was treated courteously by the front desk staff, and when I was in the kennels every single employee I spoke to (and it was quite a few over time) went out of his or her way to get information for me or to have me meet potential adoptees, and to help introduce the two service animals we already have to the new dogs to see how they got along. When I went back to the Coachella Valley Campus to license our new addition with proof of follow-up rabies vaccination -- again, I was treated courteously and efficiently.

I truly hope anyone looking to adopt a dog or cat check out the shelter.  It took me a few visits to find the right pup but you might get lucky at the first visit... or the second.

Don't buy!  Adopt!!!  Every dog that's purchased means that somewhere another awesome dog is going to be euthanized (Coachella is a no-kill shelter, thank goodness).< /review>

<user_id>111123456118714525603</user_id><user_name>Jenn McDonald<//user_name><Time>1485193410878< /Time>< rate>
1<//rate>
< review>
0 stars if i could. We adopted a dog from this place a few days ago. Firstly, they seemed to be rushing us. We had a visit with the dog and they came in and asked if we were done and wanted the dog gone before even asking if we had any questions about her. We really liked her so we went through with paperwork, the only thing they informed us about her was she was iffy about other animals, which was fine. We got her home and i started brushing her and black crumps started coming up on the brush, and a lot of it. At first i thought it was dirt, but i got suspicious of fleas eventually, and i pulled out her paperwork to reveal she was treated for fleas twice while she was there, they didnt care to tell us! She was filthy, full of dead fleas and flea dirt.. She was recently spayed so we were told not to bathe her for 10days due to stitches and recovery. So i tried to clean her as much as possible with just combing. Next morning i was combing her all out again and wanted to check her ears to make sure they were clean and at first glance I quickly noticed a odd brown thing. Closer look it was a big tick!  Must have been there for a few weeks. During their initial exams on her and pre surgery exams they should have noticed it on her and removed it. We got it out, but were very upset that these people were so neglectful. Day 3, was walking her in the morning, she had a poop and i see worms!!! The poor thing has worms as well. 3 days of having this dog and we're nursing her back to health. She is the sweestest thing and we regret nothing. But these people neglected this dog and neglected to inform us of her medical history, and didn't properly care for this dog. I 100% support adopting shelter dogs, giving a dog a second chance, but i also expect a place to care well for those dogs. It makes me think of all the other poor dogs there that could have underlying issues that arent being cared for properly. Very disappointed and wont be back there. I pray for the health of all those animals, and expect better things from that facility.< /review>

Let me begin with telling a little about myself. I am a car audio enthusiast. I have had 4 car audio show cars. My last show car won awards in every show it was entered into. I designed the system myself although it was collaborated with an engineer at G&S Designs (A very high-end speaker and amp company years ago) and an award-winning installer (Keith Davies). I was sponsored by G&S Designs, Clarion and Street Wires. My car was shown by one of the three sponsors for 3 years in a row at the CES show in Las Vegas. I myself because of my experience and being known in the car audio world in So.Cal was an official ISACA (International Sound Challenge Association)¬†¬†judge.
So, that all being said, as I recently just moved back to the US and my car had been in storage for 15 years where most of the existing sound system had unfortunately deteriorated.¬†¬†I had International replace the head unit, take out all the existing amps, crossovers etc. They did a good job with it. This was not an easy task as the car had spent the first 3 months of its life after the dealership in the stereo shop custom installing the show car system. With the installation of the new head unit and amp done, I moved to Vegas.
So, make a long story short, there is a problem with either the head unit or amp. Either hardware or installation. This problem is intermittent. When I went back to LA, I went to international to talk about the system. I was able to describe it well but as the issue is intermittent, I was not able to reproduce it when at the shop. International just talked to me like I am a person that has no idea what I am talking about when the reality is, I know more that most of them. To be clear, I‚Äôm not an installer and do not have the required installation knowledge and equipment BUT I do know sound systems and I can and do trouble shoot to narrow down issues. I understand they were busy and in their mind business on the floor is more important than standing behind what they do and fix it. New business makes money and standing behind what they do costs money but of course as most successful businesses know that‚Äôs shortsighted and customer service and taking care of the customer through full lifecycle is of equal if not more important in the long run success. International has been around a long time. They are obviously doing something right BUT could it improve? Could they be much more successful? I avoided to many warnings that this could happen by guys I still know in the business but went with my gut and price so in that way this is my own fault using International instead of others that were recommended so I‚Äôm kicking myself in the butt now.< /review>

The Alley accommodated us for my friend's bachelorette party on a Saturday night. They let us come in when they opened (6pm) and decorate for the party to reserve our location by the dance floor and live band. They also let us keep our cupcakes in the fridge. We arrived at 9pm where everyone from the bouncer to the bartenders made us feel very special since it was the bride-to-be's special night! At the end of the night the bride was hungry and they (the waitress and bouncer) offered to walk next door to pick up a pizza we ordered, HOW kind and seriously above and beyond it was. They went out of their way to make us all feel special and welcomed. The music was awesome, and we liked how they had the live band but then also played dancing music in between too. I would recommend going here to anyone! Thank you for the great service!<//text>

< Text>
Small, but great for beginner and intermediate dirt bike riders.  Just look out for slow Jeeps some of the trails.

Don't trust Google maps if it tries to bring you in the back way on a Jeep trail.  It might be faster, but will need a 4 wheel drive if you go this way. Make sure you enter from the Ortega Highway side if you have a car, camper, or a trailer. It is a paved road all the way to the staging area.</Text>

3< /rate>
< Review>
I first heard the wildomar ohv area was open after the fire, I went on 2/23/20. The road to the spot was scenic and wasn't too rough. When I got there I noticed a sign "STOP PAY HERE," there was no personel and no kiosk to pay. I parked, started putting on my gear and saw park ranger truck approaching. The ranger gave the rider next to me a citation for not paying the $5.00 cash fee. The ranger proceeded to ask about the bike and whether it was registered or not. I had a registered and legal bike but didn't have $5.00 cash, but I was fortunate enough to meet a couple that gave me the $5.00 cash to put in an envelope, provided by the "pay here" post. After paying the fee and having evidence of doing so I felt comfortable enough to unload my bike and ride.  Overall, it's small, tight, and dangerous. Having quads, dirt bikes, and some mountain bikes all in the same area is a recipe for disaster. If you do choose to ride Wildomar OHV just remember DON'T RIDE "BLOODY JERSEY HILL!" Also, don't forget to pay the $5.00 CASH fee for each bike.< /Review>
